Source Code

These source code files are a reconstruction of Sundance, the Apollo 9 LM (Lunar Module) AGC (Apollo Guidance Computer) flight software, created from binary dumps of original core rope program modules, as follows:
  • B1 — Revision 292
  • B2 — Revision 302
  • B3 — Revision 302
  • B4 — Revision 302
  • B5 — Revision 292
  • B6 — Revision 306
This means that source code does not represent a specific historical revision of Sundance, but rather a mixture of the three released versions. Nonetheless, it is capable of flying the whole Apollo 9 mission. This source code matches the binary dumps, as closely as feasible, but 100% match is not possible, due mostly to changes in memory addresses at which code and variables were allocated in different revisions of Sundance. Refer to this list of explanations for each binary mismatch.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Sundance are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

014491,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
014492,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
014493,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of a reconstructed, mixed version of Sundance
014494,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the Lunar
014495,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 9.
014496,000007:                                                                                                  ##              No original listings of this program are available;
014497,000008:                                                                                                  ##              instead, this file was created via disassembly of dumps
014498,000009:                                                                                                  ##              of various revisions of Sundance core rope modules.
014499,000010:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
014500,000011:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
014501,000012:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
014502,000013:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-06-17 MAS  Created from Luminary 69.
014503,000014: 
014504,000015:                                                                                                  ## Sundance 306
014505,000016: 
014506,000017:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
014507,000018:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
014508,000019:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
014509,000020:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
014510,000021: 
014511,000022:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
014512,000023: 
014513,000024:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
014514,000025:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
014515,000026:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
014516,000027:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
014517,000028:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
014518,000029:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
014519,000030:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
014520,000031:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
014521,000032:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
014522,000033: 
014523,000034:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
014524,000035:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
014525,000036:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
014526,000037:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
014527,000038:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
014528,000039:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
014529,000040:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

014564,000075: 
014565,000076:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
014566,000077: 
014567,000078:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
014568,000079:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
014569,000080:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
014570,000081:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
014571,000082:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
014572,000083: 
014573,000084:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
014574,000085:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
014575,000086:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
014576,000087:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
014577,000088: 
014578,000089:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
014579,000090:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
014580,000091:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
014581,000092:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
014582,000093:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
014583,000094: 
014584,000095:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
014585,000096:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
014586,000097:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
014587,000098:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
014588,000099:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
014589,000100:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
014590,000101:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
014591,000102:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
014592,000103:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
014593,000104:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
014594,000105:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
014595,000106:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
014596,000107:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
014597,000108:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
014598,000109: 
014599,000110:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
014600,000111:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
014601,000112:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
014602,000113: 
014603,000114: 
014604,000115:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
014605,000116: 
014606,000117:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
014607,000118:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
014608,000119:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
014609,000120: 
014610,000121:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
014611,000122:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
014612,000123:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
014613,000124:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
014614,000125:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
014615,000126:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
014616,000127:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
014617,000128: 
014618,000129:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
014619,000130:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
014620,000131: 
014621,000132: 
014622,000133:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
014623,000134: 
014624,000135:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
014625,000136:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
014626,000137:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
014627,000138:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
014628,000139: 
014629,000140: 
014630,000141:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
014631,000142: 
014632,000143:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
014633,000144:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
014634,000145:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
014635,000146:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
014636,000147: 
014637,000148:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
014638,000149:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
014639,000150: 
014640,000151: 
014641,000152:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
014642,000153: 
014643,000154:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
014644,000155:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
014645,000156: 
014646,000157:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
014647,000158:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
014648,000159:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
014649,000160:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
014650,000161: 
014651,000162:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
014652,000163:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
014653,000164: 
014654,000165:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
014655,000166:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
014656,000167:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
014657,000168:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
014658,000169: 
014659,000170:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
014660,000171:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
014661,000172: 
014662,000173:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
014663,000174:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
014664,000175: 
014665,000176:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
014666,000177: 
014667,000178:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
014668,000179:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
014669,000180:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
014670,000181:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
014671,000182: 
014672,000183:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
014673,000184:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
014674,000185: 
014675,000186:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
014676,000187:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
014677,000188: 
014678,000189: 
014679,000190:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
014680,000191:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
014681,000192:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
014682,000193:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

014701,000212: 
014702,000213: 
014703,000214:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014704,000215: 
014705,000216:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
014706,000217:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
014707,000218:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
014708,000219:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
014709,000220:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
014710,000221:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
014711,000222:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
014712,000223:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014713,000224:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014714,000225:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
014715,000226:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
014716,000227:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
014717,000228:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
014718,000229:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
014719,000230:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
014720,000231:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
014721,000232:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
014722,000233:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
014723,000234:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
014724,000235:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
014725,000236:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN

014727,000238:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1

014730,000241:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
014731,000242:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
014732,000243:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
014733,000244:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
014734,000245:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
014735,000246:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
014736,000247:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
014737,000248:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
014738,000249:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
014739,000250:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
014740,000251:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014741,000252:

014803,000314: 
014804,000315:                                                                                                  #  TEM5     ERASE                  EXEC TEMP
014805,000316:                                                                                                  #  NOUNADD  =      TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
014806,000317: 
014807,000318:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM  ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
014808,000319:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
014809,000320:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014810,000321:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
014811,000322:                                                                                                  #  IDAD2TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014812,000323:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
014813,000324:                                                                                                  #  IDAD3TEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN)
014814,000325:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
014815,000326:                                                                                                  #  RUTMXTEM ERASE                  TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY(MIXNN ONLY)
014816,000327:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014817,000328: 
014818,000329: 
014819,000330:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
014820,000331: 
014821,000332:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
014822,000333:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
014823,000334:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
014824,000335:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
014825,000336:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
014826,000337:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
014827,000338: 
014828,000339: 
014829,000340:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014830,000341: 
014831,000342:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT   ERASE                  COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
014832,000343:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK   ERASE                  BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
014833,000344:                                                                                                  #                                                                          RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
014834,000345:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014835,000346: 
014836,000347: 
014837,000348:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014838,000349: 
014839,000350:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP1 =      WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
014840,000351:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM =      WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
014841,000352:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP2 =      RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
014842,000353:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
014843,000354: 
014844,000355:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
014845,000356:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
014846,000357:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
014847,000358:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
014848,000359:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
014849,000360:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
014850,000361:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
014851,000362:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
014852,000363:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
014853,000364:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
014854,000365:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
014855,000366:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

014857,000368: 
014858,000369: 
014859,000370:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
014860,000371:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
014861,000372:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
014862,000373:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
014863,000374:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
014864,000375:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
014865,000376: 
014866,000377:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
014867,000378:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
014868,000379:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
014869,000380:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
014870,000381:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
014871,000382:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
014872,000383: 
014873,000384:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
014874,000385:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
014875,000386:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
014876,000387:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
014877,000388:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
014878,000389:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
014879,000390:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
014880,000391:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
014881,000392:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
014882,000393:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
014883,000394:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
014884,000395:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
014885,000396: 
014886,000397: 
014887,000398:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
014888,000399: 
014889,000400:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
014890,000401:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
014891,000402:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
014892,000403:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
014893,000404:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
014894,000405:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)
014895,000406:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
014896,000407:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
014897,000408:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
014898,000409:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
014899,000410:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
014900,000411:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
014901,000412:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
014902,000413:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
014903,000414: 
014904,000415: 
014905,000416:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
014906,000417:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
014907,000418:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
014908,000419:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
014909,000420:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
014910,000421:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
014911,000422:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
014912,000423:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
014913,000424:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
014914,000425:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
014915,000426:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
014916,000427:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
014917,000428: 
014918,000429: 
014919,000430:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
014920,000431: 
014921,000432:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
014922,000433:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
014923,000434:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
014924,000435:

015612,001123: 41,2350           04157        GOALMCYC           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  NEEDED BECAUSE BANKJUMP CANT HANDLE F/F.
015613,001124: 
015614,001125: 
015615,001126: 41,2351           04674        GODSPALM           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015616,001127: 41,2352           61533                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
015617,001128: 
015618,001129:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
015619,001130:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
015620,001131:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
015621,001132:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
015622,001133:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
015623,001134:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
015624,001135: 
015625,001136:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
015626,001137:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
015627,001138: 
015628,001139:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
015629,001140: 
015630,001141:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
015631,001142:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
015632,001143:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
015633,001144: 
015634,001145:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
015635,001146:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
015636,001147:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
015637,001148:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
015638,001149:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
015639,001150:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
015640,001151: 
015641,001152:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
015642,001153:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
015643,001154:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
015644,001155:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
015645,001156:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
015646,001157: 
015647,001158:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
015648,001159:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
015649,001160:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
015650,001161:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
015651,001162:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
015652,001163:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
015653,001164:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
015654,001165:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
015655,001166: 
015656,001167: 
015657,001168:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
015658,001169:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
015659,001170:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
015660,001171: 
015661,001172: 
015662,001173:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
015663,001174:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
015664,001175: 
015665,001176:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
015666,001177:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
015667,001178: 
015668,001179:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
015669,001180: 41,2353           45025        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
015670,001181: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
015671,001182: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
015672,001183: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2

015976,001487:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
015977,001488:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED). THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN

016186,001697:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
016187,001698:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
016188,001699:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS. IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
016189,001700:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO .  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
016190,001701:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
016191,001702:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

016781,002292: 42,3561           55042                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #   IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD
016782,002293: 42,3562           04157                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #   VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
016783,002294: 42,3563                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
016784,002295: 
016785,002296:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
016786,002297:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
016787,002298:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
016788,002299:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
016789,002300:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
016790,002301: 
016791,002302:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
016792,002303:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
016793,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
016794,002305:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
016795,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
016796,002307:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
016797,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
016798,002309: 
016799,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
016800,002311:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
016801,002312:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
016802,002313: 
016803,002314:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
016804,002315:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
016805,002316: 
016806,002317:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
016807,002318:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
016808,002319: 
016809,002320:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

016937,002448:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
016938,002449:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
016939,002450:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
016940,002451: 
016941,002452:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
016942,002453: 
016943,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
016944,002455:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
016945,002456:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
016946,002457:

016948,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E

017360,002871: 
017361,002872:                                                                                                  #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
017362,002873:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
017363,002874:                                                                                                  #   DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE. SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS,PLEASE PERFORM,
017364,002875:                                                                                                  #   OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
017365,002876: 
017366,002877: 40,3561           45030        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
017367,002878: 40,3562           03545                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
017368,002879: 
017369,002880: 
017370,002881:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
017371,002882:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
017372,002883: 
017373,002884:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
017374,002885: 
017375,002886:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
017376,002887: 
017377,002888:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
017378,002889:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
017379,002890:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
017380,002891:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
017381,002892: 
017382,002893:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
017383,002894:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
017384,002895:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
017385,002896: 
017386,002897:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
017387,002898:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
017388,002899:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
017389,002900:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
017390,002901:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
017391,002902:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
017392,002903:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
017393,002904:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
017394,002905:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
017395,002906:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
017396,002907:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
017397,002908: 
017398,002909: 40,3563           45024        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
017399,002910: 40,3564           00006                           EXTEND                                         
017400,002911: 40,3565           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
017401,002912: 40,3566           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
017402,002913: 40,3567           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
017403,002914: 40,3570           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
017404,002915: 40,3571           10000                           CCS      A                                     
017405,002916: 40,3572           03601                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
017406,002917: 40,3573           04471        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
017407,002918: 40,3574           11043                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
017408,002919: 40,3575           03577                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
017409,002920: 40,3576           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
017410,002921: 40,3577           04674                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
017411,002922: 40,3600           20746                           CADR     PINBRNCH

017413,002924: 40,3602           55013                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
017414,002925: 40,3603           11043                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
017415,002926: 40,3604           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
017416,002927: 40,3605           04514                           TC       RELDSP1                               
017417,002928: 40,3606           05225                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
017418,002929: 
017419,002930: 40,3607                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
017420,002931:

Sundance 292 

017422,002933: 
017423,002934:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
017424,002935:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
017425,002936:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
017426,002937:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
017427,002938:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
017428,002939: 
017429,002940:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
017430,002941:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
017431,002942:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
017432,002943: 
017433,002944:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
017434,002945:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
017435,002946: 
017436,002947:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
017437,002948:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
017438,002949:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
017439,002950:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
017440,002951:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
017441,002952: 
017442,002953:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
017443,002954:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
017444,002955:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
017445,002956:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
017446,002957: 
017447,002958:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
017448,002959:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
017449,002960:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
017450,002961:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
017451,002962:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
017452,002963:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
017453,002964:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
017454,002965: 
017455,002966:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
017456,002967:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
017457,002968: 
017458,002969:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
017459,002970:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
017460,002971: 
017461,002972:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
017462,002973:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
017463,002974: 
017464,002975:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
017465,002976:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
017466,002977:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
017467,002978:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
017468,002979:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
017469,002980:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
017470,002981:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
017471,002982: 
017472,002983:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
017473,002984:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
017474,002985:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
017475,002986:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
017476,002987:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
017477,002988:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
017478,002989:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
017479,002990:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
017480,002991:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
017481,002992:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
017482,002993: 
017483,002994:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
017484,002995:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
017485,002996: 
017486,002997:    4166                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
017487,002998: 
017488,002999:    4166                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
017489,003000:    4166           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017490,003001:    4167           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
017491,003002:    4170           35011                           CAF      BIT14                                 
017492,003003:    4171           71022                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
017493,003004:    4172           61013                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
017494,003005:    4173           10000                           CCS      A

017496,003007:    4175           35026                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
017497,003008:    4176           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
017498,003009:    4177           55040                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
017499,003010:    4200           23023                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS

017592,003103: 
017593,003104:                                                                                                  #  IF INTERNAL MACH CADR TO BE SPECIFIED, MPAC+2 WILL BE PLACED INTO
017594,003105:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS ).
